# Classic Rock

A massive classic rock playlist spanning 25 artists from the mid-1960s through the late 1980s, organized chronologically by album release date.

**Full catalog artists (17):** AC/DC, Aerosmith, Black Sabbath, Creedence Clearwater Revival, Eagles, Fleetwood Mac, Foreigner, Jimi Hendrix, Led Zeppelin, Lynyrd Skynyrd, Pink Floyd, Rush, Steve Miller Band, Styx, The Doors, The Rolling Stones, The Who

**Hits-only artists (8):** Boston, Cream, Deep Purple, Heart, Journey, Kansas, Thin Lizzy, ZZ Top

## Playlist Instructions

### Management

- The playlist is defined in this file — this is the source of truth
- Use the **playlist-creator** skill for rebuilding or updating
- Use the **apple-music-sync** skill for syncing to Apple Music
- Sync with: `node .github/skills/apple-music-sync/sync.mjs playlists/classic-rock.md --headless`

### Ordering

- Tracks are ordered by album release date, then by track number within each album
- Albums from all artists are interleaved chronologically
- Catalog artists include full albums; hits-only artists include selected timeless tracks
- Do not shuffle — the chronological album order is intentional

### Classic Rock Scope

- Pre-1990 albums only for all artists
- Full studio catalog albums for catalog artists (deluxe/expanded editions when available)
- Selected greatest hits for hits-only artists, placed at their original album's chronological position
- No duplicate songs — if a song appears on a later re-recording, only the original is included
